rajyasabha kii sadsyta ke baad agar siddhu party se bhi istifa dete hai to yah piem ke liye ek bada jhatka hoga par jis tarah siddhu or bijepi ke rishte bigadate chale ja rahe the, us lihaaz se ise kisi haroonges faisle ke rup main nahin dekha ja rahaa he
 At the same time, Kejriwal has surrounded the Punjab government badly on the issue of increasing drug trade and corruption
 punjab kii janata bhi aam aadmi party par bharosa jataati nazar aa rahi he 
 Kejriwal, who has dented the BJP in Delhi, is now pushing his head to form a government in Punjab, but Kejriwal is well aware that the party does not have any face in Punjab which is as popular as Prakash Singh Badal and Amarinder Singh
 Ho
 kejariwal jaanate hai ki siddhu behad lokapriy hai or bijepi ke saath unke rishte behad karaab hai
 That is why Kejriwal is seen playing bets on Sidhu in Punjab elections
 iske liye beete kai maheenon se kejariwal or siddhu gupt rup se ek dusre ke sampark main bhi the
 But the bigger question than leaving the Rajya Sabha membership is whether Sidhu's decision to leave BJP and join AAP is right and will you benefit or harm by declaring him as Chief Minister candidate? siddhu bhale hi raajnneeti main ek dashak se bhi zyaada samay se hon lekin is dauraan siddhu ne raajnneeti va jan seva se zyada manoranjan kii duniya ko praathamikta di he
 He has appeared in TV programs more than arguing in Parliament
 isliye kai baar amritsar ke saansad hone ke dauraan janata ne unke laapata hone ke poster lagaae hai kyonki vah vahaan bahut kam hi dekhe jate the
 Apart from this, Sidhu is an outstanding leader and openly expresses his views
 isliye shaayad kejariwal se talmail baitaane main unhen dikkat ho kyonki modi kii tarah kejariwal bhi party main apane alaava kisi or kii chalane nahin dete hai
 At the same time, Sidhu has tied up for many TV shows and sports programs in the coming years, will he cancel his programs after becoming CM candidate? Comments siddhu bhale hi ek achche vaktaa hon par unka itihaas kahata he ki vah raajnneeti ke prati itane gambhir kabhi nahin dikhe ki un par janata siem pad jaisi gambheer zimmedaari ke liye bharosa kar sake
 You may be reacting on Twitter to Sidhu's inclusion in the party as a huge political feat, and many people said that Sidhu would do better to entertain the public than to raise votes during campaigning
 siddhu agar aap kii jhaadu pakad kar apane siem banane ke sapane ko puraa na kar paae to shaayad vah apni raajnneetik pari main hameshaa ke liye clin bold ho jaayenge
 Therefore, Sidhu leaving BJP and joining AAP will not be less than a big challenge
 party ne jetali kii haar kaa zimmaa bhi siddhu par phoda
 After the election, many prominent party leaders accused Sidhu of not doing any work in his Lok Sabha constituency as an MP and spent more time hosting TV programs
 isliye janata ne naaraaz hokar bijepi ke khilaaf vot daale
 Jaitley's accusation of defeat in Amritsar added fuel to the relationship between Sidhu and the BJP
 beete do saalon se siddhu or unki patni va purv bijepi vidhayak navjot cor ne kai baar punjab ke mukhyamantri va sarkaar main apane sahyogi akali dal ko nishane par liya
 The Sidhu couple were unhappy with the Akali Dal's functioning and even complained to senior BJP leaders several times but the party ignored their views
 siddhu kii patni ne kuch maah purv ek sting kar apni hi sarkaar main ho rahe bhrashtachar ko ujagar kiya tha
 Taking a serious attack on his government, he said that red lighted vehicles in Punjab serve drugs
 isi varsh april ke maheene main navjot cor ne fasebuk post ke zariye bijepi se apane istife kaa elaan bhi kar diya tha
 On the other hand, Navjot Sidhu had said in an interview given to a TV channel some time ago that it is his biggest dream to become the Chief Minister of Punjab
 siddhu yah acchhee tarah jaanate hai ki akali or bijepi ke gathbandhan main unhen kabhi siem ummidavaar ghoshit nahin kiya jaayegaa
 The difficulties of the akali-bjp government, which are facing the public's anger in Punjab, have increased further after the Aam Aadmi Party entered the fray
 aap kii lokapriyata punjab main dinon din badhati ja rahi he or sabhi jagah yah charchaa he ki pehali baar punjab main maidan main utar rahi aap pradesh chunaav main sabase badi party ban sakati he
 Sidhu wants to fulfill his dream by contesting the Punjab elections as aap's CM candidate
 vahiin punjab chunaav ke maddenzar pradhanmantri narendra modi ke kehane par siddhu ko party ne kareeb dhai maah purv rajya sabha sadsy banaaya tha
 The PM was well aware that the anger of the people against the akali-bjp government in Punjab is increasing and in such a situation, the situation may get worse if Sidhu is sidelined
 siddhu kuch dinon purv swasthya bigadane ke kaaran aspataal main bhartee hue the tab bhi pradhanmantri modi ne twit karke unka haalchaal liya tha
 If Sidhu resigns from the party after Rajya Sabha membership, it would be a big blow for the PM but as the relationship between Sidhu and BJP was deteriorating, it is not seen as a surprise decision
 is
 vahiin drugs ke badhate kaarobaar or bhrashtachar ke mudde par kejariwal ne buree tarah punjab sarkaar ko gher rakhaa he
 The people of Punjab are also seen expressing confidence in the Aam Aadmi Party
 dilli main bijepi ko dhul chataane vaale kejariwal ab punjab main sarkaar banane ke liye edi chotii kaa jor laga rahe hai par kejariwal yah acchhee tarah jaanate hai ki party ke paas punjab main koi bhi aisa cheharaa nahin hai jo prakaash singh badal evam amarinder singh jitna lokapriy ho
 Kejriwal knows that Sidhu is very popular and his relationship with BJP is extremely bad
 isliye kejariwal siddhu par punjab chunaav main daanv khelte nazar aa rahe hai
 For this, Kejriwal and Sidhu were also secretly in contact with each other for the past several months
 lekin rajya sabha sadsyta chhodane se bada sawaal yah he ki kya siddhu kaa bijepi chhodkar aap main shaamil hone kaa faisla sahi he or kya aap ko unhen mukhyamantri ummidavaar ghoshit karne se faaydaa hoga yaa nuksaan ? Sidhu may have been in politics for more than a decade, but during this time, Sidhu has given priority to the world of entertainment more than politics and public service
 vah sansad main bahes karne se zyaada tivi kaaryakramon main thahaake lagaate hue zyaada nazar aae hai
 So, while being an MP from Amritsar many times, the public has put up posters of his disappearance as he was rarely seen there
 iske alaava siddhu ek bebaaq netaa hai or khulkar apane vichaaron ko prakat karte hai
 Therefore, he may have difficulty in keeping pace with Kejriwal because like Modi, Kejriwal also does not allow anyone other than him to run in the party
 vahiin siddhu ne aane vaale kuch saalon main kai tivi sho or sports kaaryakramon ke liye qaraar kar rakhaa he to kya vah siem ummidavaar banane ke baad apane kaaryakramon ko radd karenge ?tippaniyan Sidhu may be a good orator but his history says that he has never been so serious towards politics that the public can trust him for a serious responsibility like CM post
 aap bhale hi siddhu ke party main shaamil hone ko badi raajnneetik kaamayaabi maane par twitor par pratikriya dete hue kai logon ne kaha ki siddhu prachaar ke dauraan vot jutaney ke kaam se zyaada behatar janata kaa manoranjan karne kaa kaam karenge
 If Sidhu does not fulfill his dream of becoming CM by holding the broom of AAP, then perhaps he will be clean bold forever in his political innings
 isliye siddhu kaa bijepi chhod aap main janaa kisi badi chunauti se kam nahin hoga
 For the past two years, Sidhu and his wife and former BJP MLA Navjot Kaur have repeatedly targeted the Punjab Chief Minister and his ally Akali Dal in the government
 siddhu dampatti akali dal ke kaamkaaz se naakhush the or kai baar bijepi ke varisht netaaon se isaki shikaayat bhi kii lekin unki har baat ko party ne nazarandaaz kiya
 Sidhu's wife had exposed corruption in his own government in a sting a few months ago
 unhone apni sarkaar par gambhir nishaanaa sadhate hue kaha tha ki punjab main laal batti lagi gaadiyaan drugs supplai kaa kaam karti hai
 In the month of April this year, Navjot Kaur also announced her resignation from the BJP through a Facebook post
 vahiin navjot siddhu ne kuch samay pehle ek tivi channel ko die gaye intervyuu main kaha tha ki punjab kaa mukhyamantri bananaa unka sabase bada sapana he
 Sidhu is well aware that he will never be declared CM candidate in the alliance of Akali and BJP
 punjab main janata kaa rosh jhel rahi akali-bijepi sarkaar kii kathinaaiyaan aam aadmi party ke maidan main utarane ke baad or bad gai hai
 aap's popularity is increasing day by day in Punjab and it is discussed everywhere that AAP, which is contesting in Punjab for the first time, can become the largest party in the state elections
 siddhu aap ke siem ummidavaar ke rup main punjab chunaav main maidan main utarkar apane sapane ko puraa karnaa chaahate hai
 At the same time, Sidhu was made a member of the Rajya Sabha by the party about two and a half months ago at the behest of Prime Minister Narendra Modi in view of the Punjab elections
 piem yah acchhee tarah jaanate the ki punjab main akali-bijepi sarkaar ke khilaaf logon kaa gussa badhata ja rahaa he or agar aise main siddhu ko kinare kiya to sthiti or kharaab ho sakati he

" ' Subhash Chandra Bose made a promise to his father that he would sit in the examination of the Indian Civil Service in London
 1920 main unhone chauthaa sthaan hasil kiya or phir apni ichha puri karne ke liye nikal pade
 The very next year, he resigned from that luxurious service, saying, "only on the land of sacrifice and sacrifice can we establish our national estate
" '' bharat lautakar ve rashtriya sangram main kud pade or 1923 main bengal rajya congress ke sachiv or akhil bhartiya yuva congress ke adhyaksh bane
 By 1927, he emerged as the leader of the new youth movement along with Jawaharlal Nehru
 is andolan ne us saal simon kamishan ke khilaaf pradarshnon main bharat bhar ko jhakzorte hue ahm bhoomika adaa kii thi or apni pahchaan kaayam kii thi

 isi adhiveshan main yah maang uthi thi ki congress ke lakshya ko ''purna swaraj'' main badal diya jaae
 His health deteriorated in 1932 after his arrest in the Civil Disobedience Movement, which caused him to travel to Europe
 vahaan unhone europea siyasat, khaskar musolini ke fasiwad or soviet sangh ke sakhyawad ko kareeb se dekha
 He was impressed by both of them and started to believe that it is very important to establish a totalitarian regime to achieve basic social goals
 darasal yahi vah samay tha, jab nehru or bose ke rajnatik vichaaron main, khaskar fasiwad or najeevaad ke muddon par, tikhi daraar ubharne lagi
 Nehru was so strongly opposed to fascism that he refused to meet Mussolini when Mussolini wanted to meet him, while Bose not only met Mussolini, but was also influenced by him
 nehru hitler ke ubhaar se duniya ke liye badhate khatre ke tikhe aalochak the
 On the other hand, Bose never expressed that kind of hatred for fascism and he was quite ready to mobilize Germany and later Japan against Britain
 haalanki 1941 main soviet sangh par german hamale se ve khush nahin the or yahi vajah thi ki vah germany chhodkar japan chale gaye
 For Bose, socialism and fascism were not two opposing ends, just as they were for Nehru
 1938 main gandhiji ke purna samarthan se bose haripura adhiveshan ke liye congress ke sarvasammat adhyaksh chune gaye
 But the following year he decided to stand again and this time as his representative from the extremist faction of the Congress
 natijatan chunaav hue, jinamein bose 1,377 ke mukaable 1,580 voton se jite
 But the lines of war had drawn
 british hukumat ke saath samjhaute ke liye kaam kar rahe gandhivadi netaaon ko dakshinpanthi kahkar unhone chunauti uchhaali

 He made several attempts to intervene and persuaded Bose not to resign

 Confrontation was also of policy and of strategy
 bose gandhiji kii aguai main tatkaal sangharsh chaahate the, jabaki gandhiji ko lagata tha ki sangharsh kaa samay abhi nahin aayaa he

 aakhir main ve aaazaad ngkshahad fouj (iene) kii kaman sanbhaalane ke liye singapore gaye, jise japan ke haathon pakade gaye yuddh bandiyon ko jutakar 1941 main mohan singh ne banaaya tha
 The INA had made it clear that it will come to the front only when the Congress invites it; This anti-incumbency was not created as a center
 bose ne yah baat tab or saaf kar di, jab 6 july, 1944 ko unhone aaazaad hind radio par prasaaran main gandhiji ko sambodhit kiya

 On 7 September, Vikram Lander will land on the moon's surface
 After 45 hours, the Indian Space Research Organization (ISRO) will launch Chandrayaan-2's Vikram Lander on the moon's south pole on 7 September
 isro vaigyanik ise soft landing kah rahe hai

 saath hi pehla desh hoga jo swadeshi takanic se soft landing karegaa
 What is this soft landing after all? 
 
 ise kaise kiya jaataa he
 What is the risk in this? kya saavdhaaniyaan rakhni padati hai
 Let's know about soft landing
 
 
 aapane dekha hoga ki jab koi aadmi jahaaj se kudata he to thodi oonchai ke baad vah parachute kholkar jameen par utarataa he
 If he does not open the parachute, he can hit the ground rapidly due to the effect of the force of gravity and its weight
 isse use baari nuksaan ho saktaa he yaa uski maut ho sakati he
 But he does a soft landing because of the parachute
 aisa hi tab bhi hota he jab hawaii jahaaj kisi airport par land karata he
 The pilot of the aircraft first lands the previous wheel on the runway, then the next wheel
 isse plane kaa vajan gati kii disha main sahi tareeke se neeche aata he or landing sef hoti he
 This is also called soft landing
 isro ke purv vaigyanik vinod kumaar shrivastav ne bataaya ki parachute se kudata aadmi or plane kii landing soft landing kaa umdaa udhaaharan he
 Due to gravity, speed and weight on the earth, there are many measures for safe and soft landing
 aasmaan se kudate aadmi kaa vajan or gurutvkarshan ke prabhaav ko parachute kam karata he
 At the same time, a part of its wings is moved upward at the time of landing of the plane to reduce the speed due to friction of air
 vinod kumaar shrivastav ne bataaya ki chand par gurutvkarshan shakti dharti kii apeksha 1 / 6 kam he
 That is, the speed of falling there will increase
 vahaan vayumandal nahin he, isliye gharshan se gati kam karne kii kavayad bhi nahin kar sakate
 That is, neither can use parachutes nor landing like a plane
 vikram lander chand ke chaaron taraf 2 kimi prati second kii gati se gum rahaa he
 Ie 7200 km per hour
 is gati se vah chand kii sataha par land nahin kar saktaa
 Because there is no system to reduce its impact
 vinod kumaar shrivastav ne bataaya ki jab vikram lander 35 kimi kii oonchai se chand kii sataha par utarana shuru karegaa tab uske neeche lage paanchon ingine ko on kiya jayega
 The engines which were still working to push the Vikram lander forward, now the engines will reduce the speed of Vikram by 2 meters per second by creating pressure in the opposite direction
 landing se kuch second pehle gati jiro kar di jaaegi
 This will bring Vikram Lander down comfortably with the help of his four legs
 ye sara kaam vikram main maujuud onboard computer karegaa
 The sensors in it will look for the right and flat spot, then Vikram's landing

 Madhavrao Sadashivrao Golwalkar, known as Guruji, was the second RSS pracharak of the Rashtriya Swayamsevak Sangh
 inkaa janm 19 farvari, 1906 ko maharashtra ke ramtek main hua tha
 Learn 10 important things about them
 
 
 
 
 
 1
 1924 main nagpur ke isai mishanri kii ore se sanchalitahislaaf collejase intermediat kii pariksha paas karne ke baad golwalkar ne 1924 main banaras hindu uniwarsity main pravesh liya
 He passed the bsc and msc exams at the university
 2
 He was heavily influenced by Madan Mohan Malaviya while studying at BHU
 3
 Along with studies, he was fond of playing tennis and playing sitar-flute
 4
 He was first introduced to the Rashtriya Swayamsevak Sangh at Hedgewar's program in Banaras, where Dr
 headgavar kii vichaardhaara se kaaphi prabhavit hue
 5
 dow
 In view of his declining health, Hedgewar appointed Golwalkar to the post of 'sarkaryavak' on 13 August 1939 on the occasion of Rakshabandhan
 6
 From 1940-1973, for 33 years, he worked to expand the form of RSS
 7
 Golwalkar's ideas are found in his book 'we are Nationhood Defined' and his collection of speeches 'bunch of Thoughts'
 8
 Golwalkar died on 5 June 1973
